# Char of Accounts - JSON

#### cURL Request :

```javascript

curl -X POST https://api-staging.bgl360.com.au/fund/chartAccounts?fundId=0000000048f240bd0148f28816c80017 --header "Authorization:bearer df2f0e40-606f-4311-8066-590732fd126b"

```
